## Actors by Birth Year (Non-Obscure Only)

This list contains 3950 non-obscure actors sorted by birthday (most recent first).

### Filter Commands

```bash
# Run enrichment for all non-obscure actors
cd server && npm run backfill:cause-of-death-batch -- submit --limit 100

# Run enrichment for a specific actor by TMDB ID
cd server && npm run backfill:cause-of-death-batch -- submit --tmdb-id <tmdb_id>

# Dry run to see what would be processed
cd server && npm run backfill:cause-of-death-batch -- submit --limit 100 --dry-run
```
